an affliction of <i>tzaraat,</i><br>	he is to be brought to Aharon the priest or to one of his sons the priests.3 	The priest is to look at the affliction on the skin of the flesh;<br>	should hair in the afflicted-area have turned white, and the look of the affliction is deeper than the skin of his flesh,<br>	it is an affliction of <i>tzaraat;</i><br>	the priest is to look at it, and is to declare-him-<i>tamei</i>.4 	Now if it is a white spot on the skin of his flesh, and deeper its look is not than the skin,<br>	and the hair has not turned white,<br>	the priest is to shut up the afflicted-one for seven days.5 	The priest is to look at him on the seventh day,<br>	and here, should the affliction be at a standstill in his eyes,<br>	—the affliction not spread on the skin—<br>	the priest is to shut him up for seven days a second time.6 	The priest is to look at him on the seventh day a second time,<br>	and here, should the affliction have faded, and the affliction has not spread on the skin,<br>	the priest is to declare-him-pure<br>	—it is [only] a scab—<br>	when he scrubs his garments, he is pure.7 	But if the scab has spread, yes, spread on the skin<br>	after he has had the priest look at him, for declaring-him-pure,<br>	he is to have the priest look at him a second time.8 	The priest is to look, and here, should the scab have spread on the skin,<br>	the priest is to declare-him-<i>tamei&mdash;</i><br>	it is <i>tzaraat!</i>9 @ 	An affliction of <i>tzaraat</i>—when it shows on a human-being, and he is brought to the priest,10 	and the priest looks, and here, a white swelling is on the skin, and it has turned into white hair,<br>	with a live-patch of “live” flesh in the swelling:11 	it is mature <i>tzaraat</i> in the skin of his body,<br>	and the priest is to declare-him-<i>tamei;</i><br>	he is not to shut him up, for he is <i>tamei</i>.12 	Now if the <i>tzaraat</i> sprouts, yes, sprouts on the skin<br>	so that the <i>tzaraat</i> covers all the skin of the afflicted-one, from his head to his feet,<br>	wherever the priest’s eyes look:13 	the priest is to look, and here, should the <i>tzaraat</i> have covered all his flesh,<br>	he is to declare the afflicted-one pure<br>	—all of it has turned white,<br>	and he is pure!14 	But at the time of there reappearing on him live flesh, he is to be considered-<i>tamei</i>.15 	When the priest looks at the live flesh, he is to declare-him-<i>tamei;</i><br>	the live flesh—it is <i>tamei</i>, it is <i>tzaraat</i>.16 	Or when the live flesh recurs and turns back to white,<br>	he is to come to the priest;17 	the priest is to look at it, and here, should the affliction have turned back to white,<br>	the priest is to declare the afflicted one pure&mdash;<br>	he is pure.18 @ 	Now flesh—when there is in its skin a boil, and it heals,19 	but there is in place of the boil a white swelling or a white [and] reddish shiny-spot:<br>	he is to have the priest look at him.20 	The priest is to look, and here, should its look be lower than the skin,<br>	and its hair has turned white,<br>	the priest is to declare-him-<i>tamei;</i><br>	it is an affliction of <i>tzaraat</i>, in the boil it has sprouted.21 	But if the priest looks at it, and here, there is not in it any white hair,<br>	and it is not lower than the skin, but it has faded,<br>	the priest is to shut him up for seven days.22 	Now if it should spread, yes, spread on the skin,<br>	the priest is to declare-him-<i>tamei</i>—<br>	it is an affliction.23 	But if, under it, the affliction is at-a-standstill, not having spread,<br>	it is the inflammation of the boil;<br>	the priest is to declare-him-pure.24 @ 	Or flesh—when there is on the skin a burn by fire<br>	and on the live-patch of the burn is a shiny-spot, white [and] reddish, or white,25 	and the priest looks at it, and here, hair has turned white in the shiny-spot,<br>	and its look is deeper than the skin,<br>	it is <i>tzaraat</i>, in the burn it has sprouted;<br>	the priest is to declare-him-<i>tamei</i>—<br>	it is an affliction of <i>tzaraat!</i>26 	But if the priest looks at it, and here, there is not in the bright-spot any white hair, and lower it is not than the skin, and it has faded,<br>	the priest is to shut him up for seven days.27 	Then the priest is to look at him on the seventh day:<br>	if it has spread, yes, spread on the skin, the priest is to declare-him-<i>tamei</i>—<br>	it is an affliction of <i>tzaraat</i>.28 	But if, under it, the shiny-spot is at-a-standstill&mdash;it has not spread on the skin, and it has faded&mdash;<br>	it is a swelling from the burn;<br>	the priest is to declare-him-pure,<br>	for it is an inflammation from the burn.29 @ 	Now a man or a woman—when they have an affliction on the head or on the [site of the] beard:30 	and the priest looks at the affliction, and here, its look is deeper than the skin,<br>	and in it there is thin yellow hair,<br>	the priest is to declare-him-<i>tamei</i>—<br>	it is a scall, it is <i>tzaraat</i> of the head or of the beard.31 	But when the priest looks at the affliction of the scall, and here, its look is not deeper than the skin,<br>	and black hair there is none on it,<br>	the priest is to shut up the one afflicted with the scall for seven days.32 	Then the priest is to look at the affliction on the seventh day, and here, should the scall not have spread, and there is not in it [any] yellow hair,<br>	and the look of the scall is not deeper than the skin,33 	he is to shave himself,<br>	but the scall he is not to shave,<br>	and the priest is to shut up the scall-bearer for seven days a second time.34 	Then the priest is to look at the scall on the seventh day, and here, should the scall not have spread on the skin,<br>	and its look is not deeper than the skin,<br>	the priest is to declare-him-pure;<br>	he is to scrub his garments, and then he is pure.35 	But if the scall has spread, yes, spread on the skin, after his being-purified,36 	and the priest looks at him, and here, the scall has spread on the skin,<br>	the priest need not examine [him] for the yellow hair;<br>	he is <i>tamei</i>.37 	Now if in his eyes the scall is at-a-standstill, and black hair has sprouted in it,<br>	the scall has healed,<br>	he is pure,<br>	and the priest is to declare-him-pure.38 @ 	Now a man or a woman—<br>	when there is in the skin of their flesh shiny-spots, white shiny-spots,39 	and the priest looks, and here, in the skin of their flesh [are] shiny-spots, faded [or] white,<br>	it is a rash, it has sprouted on the skin,<br>	he is pure.40 @ 	Now a man—when his head becomes smooth, he is bald,<br>	he is pure.41 	And if on the edge of his face his head becomes smooth, he is forehead-bald;<br>	he is [still] pure.42 	But when there is on the bald spot or on the forehead an affliction, white [and] reddish,<br>	it is sprouting <i>tzaraat</i>, on his bald spot or on his forehead.43 	The priest is to look at him, and here, [if] the swelling of the affliction is white [and] reddish, on his bald spot or on his forehead,<br>	like the look of <i>tzaraat</i> on the skin of flesh:44 	he is a man with <i>tzaraat</i>, he is <i>tamei</i>;<br>	[yes], <i>tamei</i>, <i>tamei</i> shall the priest [declare] him, on his head is his affliction.45 	Now the one with <i>tzaraat</i> that has the affliction,<br>	his garments are to be torn,<br>	his head is to be made-bare,<br>	and his upper-lip is to be covered;<br>	<i>Tamei! Tamei!</i> he is to cry out.46 	All the days that the affliction is on him, he shall remain-<i>tamei;</i><br>	<i>tamei</i> is he,<br>	alone shall he stay, outside of the camp is his staying-place.47 @ 	Now a cloth:<br>	when there is on it an affliction of <i>tzaraat,</i><br>	on a cloth of wool or a cloth of linen,48 	or in the woof or in the warp of the linen or of the wool,<br>	or in an animal-skin or in anything worked of skin:49 	if the affliction is greenish or reddish on the cloth or the skin, or on the woof or on the warp, or in any vessel of skin,<br>	it is an affliction of <i>tzaraat,</i><br>	and he is to have the priest look at it.50 	[When] the priest looks at the affliction,<br>	he is to shut up the afflicted-item for seven days;51 	he is to look at the affliction on the seventh day;<br>	if the affliction has spread on the cloth or on the woof or on the warp or on the skin,<br>	for whatever might be done with the skin for work:<br>	the affliction is acute <i>tzaraat,</i><br>	it is <i>tamei</i>.52 	It is to be burned, the cloth, or the woof or the warp in the wool or in the linen, or in any vessel of skin that has in it any affliction,<br>	for it is acute <i>tzaraat,</i> in fire it is to be burned.53 	But if the priest looks, and here, the affliction has not spread in the cloth<br>	—whether in the woof or in the warp, or in any vessel of skin—54 	the priest is to command that they scrub that which contains the affliction,<br>	and he is to shut it up for seven days a second time.55 	The priest is to look, after the afflicted-thing has been scrubbed, and here,<br>	should the affliction not have changed its aspect, the affliction not have spread—<br>	it is <i>tamei,</i> in fire you are to burn it;<br>	it is decay, on its “bald-spot” or on its “forehead.”56 	But if the priest looks, and here, the affliction has faded, after it has been scrubbed,<br>	he is to tear it from the cloth or from the skin or from the woof or from the warp,57 	and if it is seen again on the cloth—whether in the woof or in the warp, or in any vessel of skin,<br>	it is a sprouting-thing, in fire you are to burn it, anything in which there is the affliction.58 	But the cloth or the woof or the warp or any vessel of skin that you have scrubbed, so that the affliction disappears from them,<br>	when it is scrubbed a second time,<br>	then it is pure.59 @ 	This is the Instruction [regarding] the affliction of <i>tzaraat</i> in cloth of wool or linen, or the warp or the woof, or any vessel of skin,<br>	for declaring-it-purified or for declaring-it-<i>tamei</i>.14:1 @ 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> spoke to Moshe, saying:2 	This is to be the Instruction [regarding] the one-with-<i>tzaraat,</i> at the time of his being purified:<br>	he is to be brought to the priest.3 	The priest is to go outside the camp;<br>	the priest is to look, and here, should the affliction of <i>tzaraat</i> have healed on the one-with-<i>tzaraat,</i>4 	the priest is to command that they take for the one-to-be-purified two birds, live, pure,<br>	and wood of cedar and scarlet of the worm and hyssop.5 	Then the priest is to command that they slaughter the one bird<br>	in an earthen vessel, [held] above living water,6 	and the live bird—he is to take it, and the cedar wood, the scarlet of the worm and the hyssop,<br>	and is to dip them and the live bird in the blood of the slaughtered bird, [held] above living water.7 	Then he is to sprinkle [it] over the one-to-be-purified of <i>tzaraat</i> seven times, and declare-him-pure,<br>	and is to send out the live bird into the open field.8 	The one-being-purified is to scrub his garments, shave his entire [head of] hair and wash in water,<br>	then he is pure;<br>	afterward he may enter the camp,<br>	and stay outside his tent for seven days.9 	And it shall be on the seventh day: he is to shave all his hair—his head, his beard and his eyebrows,<br>	all his body-hair he is to shave—<br>	and scrub his garments and wash his flesh in water,<br>	then he is pure.10 	On the eighth day he is to take two lambs, wholly-sound, and one lamb in its [first] year, wholly-sound,<br>	and three tenth-measures of flour as a grain-gift, mixed with oil, and one <i>log</i> of oil.11 	The priest making-purification is to stand the man to-be-purified and them<br>	before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>, at the entrance to the Tent of Appointment;12 	the priest is to take the one lamb and is to bring it near as an <i>asham</i>-offering, with the <i>log</i> of oil,<br>	and is to elevate them as an elevation-offering, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>.13 	Then he is to slaughter the lamb in the place where one slaughters the <i>hattat</i>-offering and the offering-up,<br>	in a holy place,<br>	for like the <i>hattat</i>-offering, the <i>asham</i>-offering is the priest’s,<br>	it is a holiest holy-portion.14 	Then the priest is to take some of the blood of the <i>asham</i><br>	and the priest is to place it on the ridge of the right ear of the one-being-purified, and on the thumb of his right hand, and on the thumb-toe of his right foot.15 	And the priest is to take some of the <i>log</i> of oil and is to pour it on the left palm of the priest.16 	Then the priest is to dip his right finger in some of the oil that is on his left palm<br>	and is to sprinkle some of the oil with his finger, seven times, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>.17 	From the remainder of oil that is on his palm, the priest is to place some on the ridge of the right ear of the one-being-purified, and on the thumb of his right hand, and on the thumb-toe of his right foot,<br>	on top of the blood of the <i>asham</i>-offering.18 	And what remains of the oil that is on the palm of the priest<br>	he is to place upon the head of the one-being-purified;<br>	then the priest is to effect-purgation for him, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>.19 	Then the priest is to make the <i>hattat</i>-offering and is to effect-purgation for the one-being-purified from his <i>tum’a</i>,<br>	and afterward he is to slaughter the offering-up.20 	And the priest is to offer-up the offering-up and the grain-gift upon the altar,<br>	and the priest is to effect-purgation for him;<br>	then he is pure.21 	But if he is poor and his hand does not reach [far],<br>	he is to take one lamb as an <i>asham,</i> for elevating, for effecting-purgation for him,<br>	and one tenth-measure of flour, mixed with oil, as a grain-gift, and a <i>log</i> of oil,22 	and two turtledoves or two young pigeons, [as far as] his hand can reach,<br>	the one shall be the <i>hattat</i>-offering and the other, the offering-up.23 	He is to bring them on the eighth day of his being-purified, to the priest,<br>	to the entrance of the Tent of Appointment, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>.24 	Then the priest is to take the lamb of <i>asham</i>-offering and the <i>log</i> of oil,<br>	and the priest is to elevate them as an elevation-offering, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>;25 	he is to slaughter the lamb of <i>asham</i>-offering,<br>	then the priest is to take some of the blood of the oil the priest is to pour out on the left palm of the priest;27 	the priest is to sprinkle with his right finger some of the oil that is on his left palm, seven times, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>.28 	Then the priest is to place some of the oil that is on his palm<br>	on the ridge of the right ear of the one-being-purified, and on the thumb of his right hand, and on the thumb-toe of his right foot,<br>	on the place of the blood of the <i>asham</i>-offering;29 	what-is-left of the oil that is on the palm of the priest he is to place on the head of the-one-being-purified,<br>	to effect-purgation for him, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>.30 	Then he is to make [as sacrifice] one of the turtledoves or the young pigeons, from [within] what his hand can reach31 	—whatever his hand can reach—<br>	the one as a <i>hattat</i>-offering and the other as an offering-up, along with a grain-gift,<br>	and the priest is to effect-purgation for the one-being-purified, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>.32 	This is the Instruction [regarding] the one who has an affliction of <i>tzaraat,</i><br>	whose hand cannot reach [means] for his purification.33 @ 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> spoke to Moshe and to Aharon, saying:34 	When you enter the land of Canaan, that I am giving you as a holding,<br>	and I place an affliction of <i>tzaraat</i> on a house in the land of your holding,35 	there shall come the one whose house it is<br>	and report to the priest, saying:<br>	[Something] like an affliction has been seen by me on the house!36 	Then the priest is to command that the house be cleaned before the priest enters to look at the affliction,<br>	so that nothing that is in the house becomes-<i>tamei;</i><br>	after that the priest may enter to look at the house.37 	He is to look at the affliction, and here, should the affliction be on the walls of the house [as] greenish or reddish eruptions,<br>	with their look lower than the wall,38 	the priest is to go out of the house, to the entrance of the house,<br>	and is to have the house shut up for seven days.39 	The priest is to return on the seventh day,<br>	and is to look, and here, should the affliction have spread on the walls of the house,40 	the priest is to command that they pull out the stones on which the affliction is<br>	and throw them outside the city, into a <i>tamei</i> place;41 	the house someone shall scrape inside, all around,<br>	and they are to pour the dried-mud that was scraped off outside the city, into a <i>tamei</i> place.42 	Then they are to take other stones and bring them in place of the [original] stones,<br>	other dried-mud they are to take, and are to replaster the house.43 	Now if the affliction returns and sprouts in the house<br>	after one has pulled out the stones,<br>	and after the house’s being-scraped, and after its having-been-plastered,44 	the priest is to enter,<br>	and look, and here, should the affliction have spread in the house,<br>	it is acute <i>tzaraat</i> in the house, it is <i>tamei</i>.45 	Then one is to demolish the house—its stones, its wood and all the dried-mud on the house,<br>	and one is to take [it] outside the town, to a <i>tamei</i> place.46 	One who enters the house [during] all the days of its being shut up<br>	is to remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset;47 	one lying in the house is to scrub his garments;<br>	one eating in the house is to scrub his garments.48 	Now if the priest should enter, yes, enter<br>	and look, and here, the affliction has not spread through the house<br>	after the replastering of the house,<br>	the priest is to declare the house pure, since the affliction has healed.49 	He is to take, to decontaminate the house, two birds,<br>	and cedar wood, scarlet of the worm, and hyssop,50 	and he is to slaughter the one bird in an earthen vessel, over living water;51 	then he is to take the cedar wood and the hyssop and the scarlet of the worm, and the live bird,<br>	and is to dip them in the blood of the slaughtered bird, and in the living water,<br>	and is to sprinkle [it] on the house seven times.52 	So he is to decontaminate the house with the blood of the bird and with the living water,<br>	with the live bird, with the cedar wood, with the hyssop and with the scarlet of the worm;53 	then he is to send-free the live bird, outside the town, toward the open field.<br>	When he effects-purgation for the house,<br>	then it is pure.54 @ 	This is the Instruction [regarding] any affliction of <i>tzaraat,</i> for scalls,55 	for <i>tzaraat</i> of cloth or of a house,56 	for swelling, for scabs or for shiny-spots,57 	to provide-instruction, at the time of the <i>tamei</i> and at the time of the pure.<br>	This is the Instruction [regarding] <i>tzaraat</i>.15:1 @ 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> spoke to Moshe and to Aharon, saying:2 	Speak to the Children of Israel and say to them:<br>	Any-man, any-man, when he becomes one-with-a-flow from his “flesh,”<br>	his flow—it is <i>tamei</i>.3 	And this is his <i>tum’a</i> during his flow,<br>	[whether] his “flesh” oozes with his flow or his “flesh” is sealed up by his flow,<br>	it is his <i>tum’a:</i>4 	any place-of-lying that the one-with-a-flow lies on becomes <i>tamei</i>,<br>	and any vessel that he sits on becomes <i>tamei</i>.5 	A man that touches his place-of-lying is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.6 	One who sits on the vessel on which the one-with-the-flow sits<br>	is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.7 	One who touches the flesh of the one-with-the-flow<br>	is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.8 	Now if one-with-a-flow spits on one [who is] pure,<br>	[that one] is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.9 	Any saddle-mounting that one-with-a-flow mounts, becomes-<i>tamei</i>.10 	Anyone who touches anything that is under him<br>	will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset,<br>	one-who-carries them is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.11 	Anyone whom the one-with-the-flow touches, and he did not rinse his hands in water,<br>	is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.12 	And an earthen vessel that the one-with-a-flow touches is to be broken,<br>	and any wooden vessel is to be rinsed in water.13 	Now when the one-with-a-flow is purified from his flow,<br>	he is to number himself seven days of being pure;<br>	when he scrubs his garments and washes his flesh in living water,<br>	then he is pure.14 	On the eighth day he is to take himself two turtledoves or two young pigeons<br>	and is to come before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>, at the entrance to the Tent of Appointment,<br>	and is to give them to the priest.15 	The priest is to make them [as sacrifice], the one as a <i>hattat</i>-offering and the other as an offering-up;<br>	thus will the priest effect-purgation for him before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>, from his flow.16 @ 	Now a man, when there goes out from him an emission of seed,<br>	he is to wash in water all of his flesh,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.17 	Any garment or any animal-skin on which there is an emission of seed<br>	is to be scrubbed in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.18 	And [also] a woman with whom a man lies, [with] an emission of seed:<br>	they are to wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.19 @ 	A woman—when she is one-with-a-flow, her flow being of blood from her “flesh,”<br>	seven days shall she remain in her [state of] discharge.<br>	Anyone who touches her is to remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.20 	Anything that she lies upon in her [state of] discharge becomes <i>tamei,</i><br>	anything that she sits upon becomes <i>tamei</i>.21 	Anyone who touches her lying-place is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.22 	Anyone who touches any vessel that she sat upon is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.23 	Whether it is upon the lying-place or upon the vessel that she has sat upon,<br>	on touching it he will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.24 	And if a man lies, yes, lies with her, so that her [state of] discharge is upon him,<br>	he will remain-<i>tamei</i> for seven days;<br>	any place-of-lying upon which he lies becomes <i>tamei</i>.25 @ 	Now a woman—when the flow of her blood flows for many days, when it is not the time of her discharge,<br>	or when it flows out over-and-above her discharge,<br>	all the days of her <i>tamei</i> flow she shall be like [during] the days of her discharge;<br>	she is <i>tamei</i>.26 	Any lying-place upon which she lies, all the days of her flow, shall be for her like the lying-place [during] her discharge,<br>	and any vessel that she sits upon shall be <i>tamei,</i> like the <i>tum’a</i> of her discharge.27 	Whoever touches them becomes <i>tamei</i>;<br>	he is to scrub his garments and wash in water,<br>	and will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.28 @ 	Now when she is the Purgation-Cover<i>,</i> and before the Purgation-Cover.16 	So he is to effect-purgation for the Holy-Shrine<br>	from the <i>tum’ot</i> of the Children of Israel, from their transgressions, for all of their sins,<br>	and thus he is to do with the Tent of Appointment, which dwells with them in the midst of their <i>tum’ot</i>.17 	No human is to be in the Tent of Appointment when he enters it <i>tum’ot</i> of the Children of Israel.20 	[When] he has finished purging the Holy-Shrine and the Tent of Appointment and the altar,<br>	he is to bring near the live hairy [goat],21 	Aharon is to brother!15 	By the number of years after the Homebringing<br>	you are to purchase [it] from your fellow,<br>	by the number of years of produce [left] he is to sell it to you:16 	according to the many years [left], you may charge-him-much for his purchase,<br>	according to the few years [left], you may charge-him-little for his purchase,<br>	since a [certain] number of harvests is what he is selling to you.17 	So you are not to maltreat any-man his fellow,<br>	rather, you are to hold your God in awe,<br>	for I am <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God!18 	You are to observe my laws,<br>	my regulations you are to keep, and observe them,<br>	that you may be settled on the land in security,19 	that the land may give forth its fruit<br>	and that you may eat to being-satisfied,<br>	and be settled in security upon it.20 	Now if you should say [to yourselves]:<br>	What are we to eat in the seventh year?<br>	—[for] here, we may not sow, we may not gather our produce!21 	Then I will dispatch my blessing for you during the sixth year<br>	so that it yields produce for three years;22 	you may sow the eighth year[’s yield], but you must eat of the old produce until the ninth year;<br>	until its produce comes in, you must eat what-is-old.23 	But the land is not to be sold in-harness, for the land is mine&mdash;<br>	for you are sojourners and resident-settlers with me;24 	throughout all the land of your holdings, you are to allow for redemption of the land.25 @ 	When your brother sinks down [in poverty] and has to sell some of his holding,<br>	his redeemer nearest-in-kin to him is to come<br>	and redeem the sold-property of his brother.26 	Now a man—if he has no redeemer,<br>	but his hand reaches [means] and finds enough to redeem with,27 	he is to reckon the years since its sale,<br>	and return the surplus to the man to whom he sold it,<br>	and it is to return to his holding.28 	But if his hand does not find enough [means] for returning it,<br>	what he sold is to remain in the hand of the one purchasing it, until the Year of Homebringing;<br>	it is to go-free in the Homebringing-Year, and it is to return to his holding.29 	A man—if he sells a residential house in a walled town,<br>	its redemption-period until the end of the year of its sale;<br>	a year-of-days shall be its redemption-period.30 	If it is not redeemed before a whole year of it has been fulfilled,<br>	the house that is in the town that has a wall shall be established, in-harness, for him who purchases it, throughout his generations;<br>	it is not to go-free in the Homebringing-Year.31 	But houses in villages that do not have a wall around them,<br>	as open-fields of the land are they to be reckoned;<br>	there may be redemption for them,<br>	and in the Homebringing-Year they may go free.32 	Now [as for] the towns of the Levites, the houses in the towns of their holding—<br>	redemption-right for the ages is to belong to the Levites.33 	[That] which is redeemed from the Levites:<br>	it is to go free, the house sold in the town of their holding, in the Homebringing-Year,<br>	for houses of Levitical towns, they are their holding amid the Children of Israel.34 	But pasture-land of the field [near] their towns is not to be sold,<br>	for it is a holding for the ages for them.35 @ 	Now when your brother sinks down [in poverty]<br>	and his hand falters beside you,<br>	then shall you hold him<br>	as [though] a sojourner and resident-settler,<br>	and he is to live beside you.36 	Do not take from him biting-interest or profit,<br>	but hold your God in awe,<br>	that your brother may live beside you!37 	Your silver you are not to give him at interest,<br>	for profit you are not to give [him] your food;38 	I <sc>Yhwh</sc> am your God<br>	who brought you out of the land of Egypt<br>	to give you the land of Canaan,<br>	to be a God for you!39 @ 	And when your brother sinks down [in poverty] beside you, and sells himself to you,<br>	you are not to make him serve the servitude of a serf&mdash;40 	as a hired-hand, as a resident-settler is he to be beside you;<br>	[only] until the Year of Homebringing is he to serve beside you.41 	Then he is to go-free from beside you,<br>	he and his children beside him;<br>	he may return to his clan,<br>	and to the holding of his fathers he may return.42 	For my servants are they<br>	whom I brought out of the land of Egypt;<br>	they are not to be sold as the sale of serfs.43 	You are not to dominate him with crushing-labor;<br>	rather, you are to hold your God in awe!44 @ 	Your servant and your maid that belong to you from the nations surrounding you, from them you may purchase serf and maid;45 	also from the sons of the residents who sojourn beside you, from them dominate him with crushing-labor before your eyes.54 	And if he has not been redeemed in [any of] these [ways],<br>	he is to go free in the Year of Homebringing, he and his children beside him.55 	For it is to me that the Children of Israel are servants&mdash;<br>	my servants are they,<br>	whom I brought out of the land of Egypt,<br>	I am <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God!26:1 @ 	You are not to make for yourselves no-gods,<br>	a carved-image or a standing-pillar you are not to establish for yourselves,<br>	a decorated stone you are not to place in your land, to bow down to it,<br>	for I <sc>Yhwh</sc> am your God!2 	My Sabbaths you are to keep, my Holy-Shrine you are to hold-in-awe;<br>	I am <sc>Yhwh</sc>!3 @ 	If by my laws you walk, and my commands you keep, and observe them,4 	then I will give-forth your rains in their set-time,<br>	so that the earth gives-forth its yield<br>	and the trees of the field give-forth their fruit.5 	Threshing will overtake vintage for you, and vintage will overtake sowing;<br>	you shall eat your food to being-satisfied, and be settled in security in your land.6 	I will give peace throughout the land, so that you will lie down with none to make you tremble,<br>	I will cause-to-cease wild beasts from the land, and a sword shall not cross through your land.7 	You shall pursue your enemies, and they will fall before you to the sword;8 	five of you will pursue a hundred, and a hundred of you, a myriad pursue,<br>	and your enemies will fall before you to the sword.9 	I will turn-my-face toward you, make-you-fruitful and make-you-many,<br>	and I will establish my covenant with you.10 	You will eat old-grain, the oldest-stored,<br>	and the old for the new you will have to clear out.11 	I will place my Dwelling in your midst,<br>	and I will not repel you.12 	I will walk about in your midst,<br>	and I will be a God for you, and you yourselves will be a people for me.13 	I <sc>Yhwh</sc> am your God<br>	who brought you out of the land of Egypt,<br>	from your being serfs to them;<br>	I broke the bars of your yoke, enabling you to walk upright!14 @ 	But if you do not hearken to me, and do not observe all these commandments,15 	if my laws you spurn, and if my regulations you repel<br>	by not observing all my commandments, by your violating my covenant,16 	I in turn will do this to you:<br>	I will mete out shock to you,<br>	and consumption, and fever,<br>	wearing out the eyes and exhausting the breath;<br>	and you will sow your seed for naught, for your enemies will eat it.17 	And I will set my face against you, you will be hit-by-plague in the face of your enemies;<br>	those who hate you will dominate you,<br>	you will flee, with no one pursuing you!18 @ 	Now if, after all that, you do not hearken to me,<br>	I will continue to discipline you, sevenfold, for your sins—19 	I will break your fierce pride!<br>	I will give your heavens to be like iron, and your earth like bronze,20 	so that your power will be spent for naught;<br>	your land will not give forth its yield,<br>	the trees of the land will not give forth their fruit.21 @ 	Now if you walk with me [in] opposition, and do not consent to hearken to me,<br>	I will continue against you blows, sevenfold, according to your sins—22 	I will send loose against you the wild-beasts of the field,<br>	so that they bereave you,<br>	so that they [utterly] cut off your animals,<br>	so that they make you few, and your roads become desolate.23 @ 	Now if, after these-things, you do not accept-discipline from me,<br>	but [continue to] walk with me [in] opposition,24 	I will walk with you, I myself, with opposition;<br>	I will strike you, yes, I myself, sevenfold for your sins:25 	I will bring against you an avenging sword, taking-vengeance for the covenant.<br>	Should you gather yourselves into your cities,<br>	I will send-free pestilence in your midst,<br>	and you will be given into the hand of your enemies.26 	When I break the “staff of bread” for you, ten women shall bake your bread in one oven;<br>	they will return your bread by weight,<br>	and you will eat, but you will not be satisfied.27 @ 	And if after this you will not hearken to me,<br>	but [still] walk with me with opposition,28 	I will walk with you in the heat of opposition;<br>	I will discipline you, even I myself, sevenfold for your sins!29 	You will eat the flesh of your sons,<br>	and the flesh of your daughters, you will eat!30 	I will wipe out your sanctuaries and and cut down your cult-stands,<br>	I will place your corpses atop the corpses of your Illicit-Things<br>	and I will repel you.31 	I will make your cities a wasteland,<br>	I will make-desolate your holy-shrines,<br>	and I will not savor your soothing savors!32 	And I, I myself, will make the land desolate,<br>	so that your enemies that settle in it will be appalled-at-the-desolation in it.33 	And you I will scatter among the nations;<br>	I will unsheath the sword against you,<br>	so that your land becomes a desolation and your cities become a wasteland.34 	Then the land will find-acceptance regarding its Sabbaths,<br>	all the days of desolation—when you are in the land of your enemies—<br>	then the land will enjoy-cessation, and find-acceptance regarding its Sabbaths.35 	All the days of desolation it will enjoy-cessation,<br>	since it did not enjoy-cessation during its Sabbaths when you were settled on it.36 	Now those that remain among you—I will bring faintness into their hearts, in the lands of their enemies,<br>	they will be set-in-pursuit by the sound of a leaf blown about,<br>	they will flee as if in flight from a sword and will fall, though there is no pursuer!37 	They will stumble, each-man over his brother, as before the sword, though pursuer there is none.<br>	And you will not be able to stand-your-ground before your enemies;38 	rather, you will perish among the nations—<br>	it will devour you, the land of your enemies.39 	Those that remain among you will rot away in their iniquity, in the lands of their enemies;<br>	yes, because of the iniquities of their fathers, with them they shall rot away.40 	Now should they confess their iniquity and the iniquity of their fathers, in their breaking-faith by which they broke-faith with me<br>	—yes, since they have walked with me in opposition,41 	yes, I myself will walk with them in opposition,<br>	and will bring them into the land of their enemies—<br>	if then their foreskinned heart should humble itself,<br>	if then they should find-acceptance regarding their iniquity,42 	I will bear-in-mind my Yaakov covenant,<br>	and yes, my Yitzhak covenant, and yes, my Avraham covenant I will bear-in-mind, and the land I will bear-in-mind.43 	—The land will have to be left behind by them, attaining-acceptance through its Sabbaths by being-desolate-of them,<br>	and they will have to find-acceptance regarding their iniquity,<br>	because, because my regulations they spurned, and my laws they repelled.—44 	And yes, even then, when they are in the land of their enemies, <br>	I will not spurn them, I will not repel them, to finish them off, to abrogate my covenant with them,<br>	for I <sc>Yhwh</sc> am their God!45 	I will bear-in-mind to their [benefit] the covenant of the former-ones<br>	whom I brought out of the land of Egypt, before the Israel at Mount Sinai, by the hand of Moshe.27:1 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> spoke to Moshe, saying:2 	Speak to the Children of Israel and say to them:<br>	Anyone—when one would make a vow-offering<br>	in your <i>shekels</i> by the Holy-Shrine <i>shekel.</i>4 	And if it is a female, your assessment shall be thirty <i>shekels.</i>5 	If the age [is] from five years up to the age of twenty years,<br>	your assessment for a male is twenty <i>shekels</i>, and for a female, ten <i>shekels.</i>6 	If from the age of a month up to the age of five years,<br>	your assessment is for a male, five silver <i>shekels,</i> and for a female, your assessment, three silver <i>shekels.</i>7 	If from the age of sixty years and upward,<br>	if a male, your assessment shall be fifteen <i>shekels,</i> and for a female, ten <i>shekels.</i>8 	If he sinks down [in poverty], lower than the assessment,<br>	he is to be stood before the priest,<br>	and the priest is to assess [the amount] for him;<br>	according to what the hand of the one-making-the-vow can reach, the priest is to assess him.9 	If [it concerns] an animal from which they bring near a near-offering for <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	all of what he gives from it to <sc>Yhwh</sc> is to be a holy-portion.10 	He is not to substitute for it and he is not to exchange it, good for ill or ill for good;<br>	if they exchange, yes, exchange animal for animal,<br>	it will be that it and its exchanged-one will be a holy-portion.11 	If it [concerns] any <i>tamei</i> animal from which there may not be brought near a near-offering for <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	the animal is to be stood before the priest,12 	and the priest is to make-assessment for it, between good and ill,<br>	according to your assessment by the priest, thus shall it be.13 	And if he [wants to] redeem, yes, redeem it,<br>	he is to add its fifth-part to your assessment.14 @ 	Now a man—when he hallows his house as holy-property to <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	the priest is to assess it, between good and ill;<br>	as the priest assesses it, thus shall [its cost] be-established.15 	And if the one-who-hallows-it would redeem his house,<br>	he is to add a fifth-part [to the] silver of your assessment,<br>	and it shall remain his.16 	If from the field of his holding any-man hallows [part] to <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	your assessment shall be according to its seed-requirement:<br>	the seed-requirement of a <i>homer</i> of barley, fifty silver <i>shekels.</i>17 	If as of the year of Homebringing he hallows his field, as your assessment [its cost] will be-established.18 	but if it is after the Homebringing that he hallows his field,<br>	the priest is to reckon for him the silver according to the years left until the Year of Homebringing,<br>	and it is to be subtracted from your [first] assessment.19 	If he wants to redeem, yes, redeem the field, the one hallowing it,<br>	he is to add a fifth-part of the silver of your assessment of it, and [its cost] is to be-established for him.20 	But if he does not want to redeem the field,<br>	or if he has sold the land to another man,<br>	it cannot be redeemed again—21 	the field shall be, when it is.25 @ 	All your assessments are to be according to the Holy-Shrine <i>shekel,</i><br>	twenty grains being the [one] <i>shekel.</i>26 	However, a firstborn that is assigned-as-firstborn to <sc>Yhwh</sc>, among animals—<br>	no man may hallow it;<br>	whether ox or sheep, it is <sc>Yhwh’s</sc>.27	Now if [it is] of a <i>tamei</i> animal, he is to redeem it at your assessment,<br>	and add its fifth-part to it,<br>	and if it is not redeemed, it is to be sold at your assessment.28 	However, everything specially-devoted that a man devotes for <sc>Yhwh</sc> from all that is his,<br>	whether of man or of beast or of field of his holding,<br>	is not to be sold and not to be redeemed;<br>	everything specially-devoted—it is a holiest holy-portion for <sc>Yhwh</sc>.29 	Anyone specially-devoted that has been devoted-to-destruction, among humans, is not to be ransomed;<br>	he is to be put to death, yes, death.30 	And every tithe of the land, [whether] from the seed of the land or from the fruit of the tree:<br>	for <sc>Yhwh</sc> it is, a holy-portion for <sc>Yhwh</sc>.31 	If a man wants to redeem, yes, redeem any of his tithes,<br>	its fifth-part he is to add comes over him15 	and he feels rage toward his wife, though she did not make-herself-<i>tamei</i>—<br>	the man is to bring his wife to the priest.<br>	He is to bring a near-offering for her: <br>	a Bringing the Bane.19 	The priest is to have her swear and is to say to the woman:<br>	If a man did not lie with you,<br>	and if you did not stray to make-yourself-<i>tamei</i> under your husband[’s thigh to fall!<br>	And the woman is to say: Amen! Amen!23 	Then the priest is to write these curses in a record<br>	and is to blot [them] into the Water of Bitterness;24 	he is to make the woman drink the Water of Bitterness Bringing the Bane,<br>	so that the Water Bringing the Bane may enter her, for “bitterness.”25 	Then the priest is to take from the hand of the woman the grain-gift of rage,<br>	he is to elevate the grain-gift before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>, <br>	and is to bring it near, to the altar.26 	The priest is to scoop out of the grain-gift its reminder-portion,<br>	and is to turn it into smoke upon the altar;<br>	after that he is to make the woman drink the water.27 	When he has had her drink the water, it shall be:<br>	if she made-herself-<i>tamei</i><br>	and broke-faith, yes, faith with her husband,<br>	the Water Bringing the Bane shall enter her, for “bitterness,”<br>	her belly shall swell and her thigh shall fall,<br>	and the woman shall become an object-of-curse among her kinsfolk.28 	But if the woman did not make-herself-<i>tamei</i><br>	and she is pure,<br>	she is to be cleared and she may-bear-seed, yes, seed.29 	This is the Instruction [regarding] cases-of-zealous-rage,<br>	when a woman strays under her husband[’s authority]<br>	and makes-herself-<i>tamei,</i>30 	or when there comes over a man a rush of zealous-rage, so that he feels rage toward his wife:<br>	he is to have the woman stand before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	and the priest is to perform regarding her [according to] all this Instruction.31 	The man shall be clear of iniquity,<br>	but that woman shall bear her iniquity.6:1 @ 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> spoke to Moshe, saying:2 	Speak to the Children of Israel and say to them:<br>	A man or a woman—when one sets oneself apart, by vowing the vow of a Nazirite/Consecrated-One, to consecrate-oneself for <sc>Yhwh</sc>:3 	from wine and from beer one is to consecrate oneself;<br>	fermentation of wine and fermentation of beer one is not to drink,<br>	any liquid of grapes one is not to drink,<br>	and grapes, moist or dried, one is not to eat.4 	All the days of one’s being consecrated,<br>	anything that is made from the vine of wine, from seeds to skin, one is not to eat.5 	All the days of one’s vow of being consecrated<br>	a razor is not to go-across one’s head;<br>	until the fulfilling of days that one is consecrated for <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	holy shall one remain;<br>	one is to grow loose the hair on one’s head.6 	All the days that one consecrates-oneself for <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	near a dead person one is not to come—7 	[even] for one’s father or one’s mother, one’s brother or one’s sister;<br>	one is not to make-oneself-<i>tamei</i> by them when they die,<br>	for [hair] consecrated for one’s God is upon one’s head.8 	All the days of one’s being-consecrated,<br>	one is holy to <sc>Yhwh</sc>.9 	Now if a dead [person] has died near one<br>	suddenly, all-of-a-sudden,<br>	so that one makes-<i>tamei</i> the consecrated [hair of one’s] head,<br>	one is to shave one’s head on the day of one’s becoming-pure;<br>	on the seventh day one is to shave it.10 	Now on the eighth day<br>	one is to bring two turtledoves or two young pigeons to the priest,<br>	to the entrance of the Tent of Appointment.11 	The priest is to make one as a <i>hattat</i>/decontamination-offering, and one as an offering-up;<br>	he is to effect-purgation for one,<br>	in that one became-contaminated by the [dead] person.<br>	One is to make one’s head holy [again] on that day,12 	and is to reconsecrate to <sc>Yhwh</sc> the days of one’s being consecrated, bringing a lamb in its [first] year as an <i>asham/compensation-offering.<br>	The former days are to be [considered] fallen-away,<br>	since one’s state-of-consecration became <i>tamei</i>.13 @ 	Now this is the Instruction [regarding] the Consecrated One:<br>	On the day that one’s days of being consecrated are fulfilled,<br>	one is to be brought to the entrance of the Tent of Appointment;14 	one is to bring near as one’s near-offering to <sc>Yhwh</sc>:<br>	a lamb in its [first] year, wholly-sound, one, as an offering-up,<br>	and one ewe-lamb in its [first] year, wholly-sound, as a <i>hattat-</i>offering, and one ram, wholly-sound, as a <i>shalom</i>-offering,15 	and a basket of <i>matzot</i> of flour, round-loaves mixed with oil,<br>	and wafers of <i>matzot</i> spread with oil,<br>	[as well as] their grain-gift and their poured-offerings.16 	The priest is to come near before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	and is to sacrifice his <i>hattat-</i>offering and his offering-up,17 	and the ram he is to make as a sacrifice of <i>shalom</i> to <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	together with the basket of <i>matzot;</i><br>	then the priest is to make his grain-gift and his poured-offering.18 	The Consecrated One is then to shave, at the entrance of the Tent of Appointment, one’s consecrated head,<br>	and is to take the hair of one’s consecrated head <br>	and put [it] on the fire that is under the sacrifice of <i>shalom.</i>19 	The priest is to take the shoulder of the ram, boiled,<br>	and one loaf of <i>matza</i> from the basket,<br>	and one wafer of <i>matza,</i><br>	and is to put [them] on the palms of the Consecrated One, after one’s shaving of one’s consecrated [hair].20 	The priest is to elevate them as an elevation-offering, before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc>—<br>	it is a holy-offering for the priest—<br>	on top of the breast of the elevation-offering and on top of the thigh of the contribution,<br>	and after [that] the Consecrated One may drink wine.21 	This is the Instruction [regarding] the Consecrated One<br>	who vows a near-offering to <sc>Yhwh</sc> in addition to one’s [requirement of] consecration,<br>	aside from what one’s hand can reach:<br>	according to the vow that one has vowed, thus is one to make, in addition to the instructed-requirements of one’s consecration.22 @ 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> spoke to Moshe, saying:23 	Speak to Aharon and to his sons, saying:<br>	Thus are you to bless the Children of Israel;<br>	say to them:<br>24 @ 		May <sc>Yhwh</sc> month,<br>	between the setting-times,<br>	you are to make it at its appointed-time;<br>	according to all its laws, according to all its regulations, you are to make it.4 	So Moshe spoke [instructions] to the Children of Israel, to make the Passover-offering.5 	And they made the Passover-offering<br>	in the first [month], on the fourteenth day of the month,<br>	between the setting-times,<br>	in the Wilderness of Sinai.<br>	Exactly as <sc>Yhwh</sc> had commanded Moshe,<br>	thus the Children of Israel did.6 	But there were some men who were <i>tamei</i> by reason of a <i>tamei</i> by reason of a [dead] human person;<br>	[but] why should we be restrained<br>	by not [being allowed] to bring near the near-offering of <sc>Yhwh</sc> in its appointed-time in the midst of the Children of Israel?8 	Moshe said to them:<br>	Stand by, and let me hear <br>	what <sc>Yhwh</sc> shall command regarding you.9 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> spoke to Moshe, saying:10 	Speak to the Children of <sc>Yhwh</sc>:11 	in the second month, on the fourteenth day, between the setting-times,<br>	he is to make it;<br>	together with<i> matza</i> and bitter-herbs they are to eat it.12 	They are not to been on a journey,<br>	and holds back from making the Passover-offering:<br>	cut off will that person be from his kinspeople,<br>	for the near-offering of Passover for <sc>Yhwh</sc> he has not brought Passover-offering and according to its regulation,<br>	thus he is to make [it].<br>	One law is there to be for you, for the sojourner and for the native of the land.15 @ 	Now at the time that the saying:2 	This is the law of the instructed-ritual<br>	that <sc>Yhwh</sc> has commanded, saying:<br>	Speak to the Children of Israel,<br>	that they may take you a red cow, wholly-sound,<br>	that has in it no defect,<br>	that has not yet yielded to a yoke;3 	you are to give it to El’azar the priest,<br>	and it is to be brought forth, outside the camp,<br>	and is to be slaughtered in his to be burned before his eyes;<br>	its hide, its flesh, and its blood<br>	along with its dung, are to be burned.6 	The priest is to take wood of cedar, and hyssop, and scarlet of worm,<br>	and is to throw [them] into the midst of the cow burning.7 	He is to scrub his garments, the priest, and is to wash his body in water,<br>	and afterward he may enter the camp,<br>	but the priest will remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.8 	And he who burned it<br>	is to scrub his garments in water and is to wash his body in water,<br>	and remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.9 	And a [ritually] pure man Undefilement;<br>	it is [for] decontamination.10 	The collector of the cow’s ashes is to scrub his garments<br>	and remain-<i>tamei</i> until sunset.<br>	It shall be for the Children of Israel and for the sojourner who sojourns in their midst <br>	as a law for the ages:11 	he who touches a dead-body of any human person<br>	[shall be deemed] <i>tamei</i> for seven days.12 	Should he decontaminate himself with it on the third day and on the seventh day, then he is pure;<br>	if he does not decontaminate himself on the third day and on the seventh day, then he is not pure.13 	Anyone who touches a dead-body of any human person who has died,<br>	and does not decontaminate himself—<br>	the Dwelling of <sc>Yhwh</sc> has he made-<i>tamei,</i><br>	cut off shall that person be from Israel,<br>	since the Waters of Undefilement were not dashed on him;<br>	<i>tamei</i> shall he be, his <i>tum’a</i> [stays] within him!14 	This is the Instruction:<br>	A human who dies in a tent—<br>	anyone who enters the tent, and anyone who is in the tent,<br>	shall be <i>tamei</i> for seven days.15 	And any open vessel that has no cover tied down on it,<br>	it is <i>tamei</i>!16 	And anyone who touches, on the [open] field,<br>	one slain by the sword or a dead-body,<br>	or human bones or a burial-place,<br>	shall be <i>tamei</i> for seven days.17 	They are to take for the <i>tamei</i> one some dust of the burned <i>hattat-</i>offering,<br>	and they are to add to it living water, in a vessel.18 	He is to take hyssop and dip it into the water, the [ritually] pure one,<br>	he is to sprinkle [it] on the Tent and on all the implements<br>	and on the persons that were there,<br>	and on the one who touched the bones or the slain one or the dead-body or the burial-place.19 	Then the pure one is to sprinkle [it] on the <i>tamei</i> one on the third day and on the seventh day,<br>	thus decontaminating him on the seventh day;<br>	then he is to scrub his garments and wash with water,<br>	and be purified after sunset.20 	Now a man who becomes-<i>tamei</i> and does not decontaminate himself—<br>	cut off shall that person be from the midst of the death the murderer,<br>	upon meeting him, he may put him to death.20 	Now if in hatred he pushed him,<br>	or threw [something] at him lying-in-wait, so that he died,21 	or in enmity struck him with <sc>Yhwh</sc> and said:<br>	My Lord <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	do not bring-ruin on your people, your inheritance<br>	whom you redeemed in your greatness,<br>	whom you took out of Egypt with a strong hand!27 cause their death in the wilderness!29 	—And they are your people, your inheritance<br>	whom you took out in your great power and with your outstretched arm!10:1 	At that time <sc>Yhwh</sc> said to me:<br>	Carve yourself two tablets of stone, like the first ones,<br>	and come up to me, on the mountain,<br>	and make yourself a Coffer of wood.2 	I will write on the tablets the words that were on the tablets, the first-ones, that you smashed,<br>	and you are to put them in the Coffer.3 	So I made a Coffer of acacia wood,<br>	I carved out two tablets of stone, like the first ones,<br>	and I went up, on the mountain, with the two tablets in my arms.4 	And he wrote on the tablets according to the first writing,<br>	the Ten Words<br>	that <sc>Yhwh</sc> spoke to you on the mountain, from the midst of the fire,<br>	on the day of the Assembly,<br>	and <sc>Yhwh</sc> gave them to me.5 	Then I faced about and came down the mountain,<br>	and I put the tablets in the Coffer that I had made,<br>	and they have remained there,<br>	as <sc>Yhwh</sc> had commanded me.6 @ 	The Children of Israel marched from the Wells of the Children of Ya’akan to Mosera;<br>	there Aharon died, and he was buried there,<br>	and El’azar his son served-as-priest in his stead.7 	From there they marched to Gudgoda,<br>	and from Gudgoda to Yotvata, a land of streams of water.8 	At that time name,<br>	until this day.9 	Therefore Levi did not have an inheritable portion along with his brothers;<br>	<sc>Yhwh</sc> is his inheritance,<br>	as <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God promised him.10 	As for upon you.11 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> said to me:<br>	Arise, go on the march before the people,<br>	so that they may enter and take possession of the land<br>	which I swore to their fathers, to give them.12 @ <sc>Yhwh</sc> has been proclaimed!3 	The foreigner you may oppress,<br>	and he who belongs to you;<br>	as for your brother, your hand is to release [him].4 	However, there will not be among you any of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,<br>	by taking care to observe all this commandment that I command you today,6 	indeed, <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God will bless you<br>	as he promised you;<br>	you will cause many nations to give-pledges,<br>	but you will not [have to] give-pledges;<br>	you will rule over many nations,<br>	but over you they shall not rule.7 @ 	When there is among you a needy one<br>	from any-one of your brothers, within one of your gates<br>	in the land that <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God is giving you,<br>	you are not to toughen your heart;<br>	you are not to shut your hand<br>	to your brother, the needy one.8 	Rather, you are to open, yes, open your hand to him,<br>	and are to give-pledge, yes, pledge to him,<br>	sufficient for his lack that is lacking to him.9 	Take you care,<br>	lest there be a word in your heart, a base one, saying:<br>	The seventh year, the Year of Release, is nearing—<br>	and your eye be set-on-ill toward your brother, the needy one,<br>	and you not give to him,<br>	so that he calls out because of you to <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	and sin be incurred by you.10 	You are to give, yes, give to him;<br>	your heart is not to be ill-disposed in your giving to him,<br>	for on account of this matter<br>	<sc>Yhwh</sc> your God will bless you in all your doings<br>	and in all the enterprises of your hand!11 	For the needy will never be gone from amidst the land;<br>	therefore I command you, saying:<br>	You are to open, yes, open your hand to your brother, to your afflicted one,<br>	and to your needy-one in your land!12 @ 	When your brother is sold to you, Hebrew-male or Hebrew-female,<br>	and serves you for six years:<br>	now in the seventh year<br>	you are to send-him-free, at liberty, from beside you.13 	Now when you send-him-free, at liberty, from beside you,<br>	you are not to send-him-free empty-handed;14 	you are to adorn, yes, adorn him<br>	from your flock, from your threshing-floor and from your vat,<br>	[from] that which <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God has blessed you, you are to give to him.15 	You must bear-in-mind<br>	that a serf were you in the land of Egypt,<br>	and <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God redeemed you&mdash;<br>	therefore I command you this word today!16 	Now it shall be<br>	if he says to you:<br>	I will not go out from beside you,<br>	for I love you and your household<br>	—for it goes-well for him beside you—17 	you are to take a piercing-tool<br>	and are to put it through his ear, into the door,<br>	and he shall be your serf forever;<br>	even to your maid you are to do thus.18 	You are not to let-it-be-hard in your eyes<br>	when you send-him-free, at liberty, from beside you,<br>	for double the hire of a hired-hand<br>	did he serve you, six years.<br>	Then <sc>Yhwh</sc> will bless you<br>	in all that you do.19 @ 	Every firstling that is born in your flock and in your herd, the male,<br>	you are to hallow to <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God;<br>	you are not to do serving-tasks with the firstling of your ox,<br>	you are not to shear the firstling of your sheep.20 	Before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God you are to eat it, year after year,<br>	in the place that <sc>Yhwh</sc> chooses—<br>	you and your household.21 	Now if there be in it a defect,<br>	lame or blind,<br>	any defect for ill,<br>	you are not to sacrifice [it] to <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God.22 	Within your gates you are to eat it,<br>	the <i>tamei</i> and the pure together,<br>	as the gazelle, so the deer.23 	Only: its blood you are not to eat;<br>	on the earth you are to pour it out, like water.16:1 @ 	Keep the month of Aviv/Ripe-Grain.<br>	You are to observe Passover to <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,<br>	for in the month of Aviv<br>	<sc>Yhwh</sc> your God took you out of Egypt, at night.2 hands,<br>	and you shall be oh so joyful!16 	[At] three points in the year<br>	are all your male-folk to be seen<br>	at the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God<br>	in the place that he chooses:<br>	on according to the giving-capacity of his hand,<br>	according to the blessing of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God that he has given you.18 @ 	Judges and officials you are to provide for yourselves, within all equitable.20 	Equity, equity you are to pursue,<br>	in order that you may live<br>	and possess the land that <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God is giving you!21 @ 	You are not to plant yourself an Ashera [or] hates.17:1 @ 	You are not to sacrifice to <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God<br>   an ox or a sheep that has on it a defect, anything ill,<br>	for it is an abomination to <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God!2 @ 	When there <sc>Yhwh</sc> his God,<br>	to be careful concerning all the words of this Instruction<br>	and these laws, to observe them,20 	that his heart not be raised above his brothers,<br>	that he not turn aside from what-is-commanded,<br>	to the right or to the left,<br>	in order that he may prolong [his] days over his kingdom,<br>	he and his sons,<br>	in the midst of Israel.18:1 @ 	There is not to be word not happen, not come-about—<br>	[then] that is the word that <sc>Yhwh</sc> did not speak;<br>	with presumption did the prophet speak it;<br>	you are not to be-in-fear of him!19:1 @ 	When break-the-neck of the she-calf there, in the wadi.5 	Then they are to approach, the priests, the Sons of Levi<br>	—for <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God has chosen them to attend on him and to give-blessing in <sc>Yhwh’s</sc> name,<br>	and by their statement shall be [settled] every legal-quarrel and every case-of-assault—6 	and all the elders of that town, the ones nearest the corpse,<br>	are to wash midst—<br>	for you are to do what is right in the eyes of <sc>Yhwh</sc>!10 @ 	When you go out to battle against your enemies<br>	and <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God gives him into your hand, and you render your land <i>tamei</i><br>	that <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God is giving you as an inheritance.22:1 @ 	You are not to see the ox of your brother or his sheep wandering off<br>	and hide yourself from your fathers, promised you.4 	Now it shall be, on your crossing the Jordan:<br>	set up these stones<br>	about which I command you today, on Mount Eval,<br>	and plaster them with plaster.5 	You are God;<br>	you are to offer-up on it offerings-up to <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God.7 	[When] you sacrifice <i>shalom</i>-offerings, you may eat [them] there,<br>	and you are to rejoice<br>	before the presence of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God.8 	And you are to write on the stones<br>	all the words of this Instruction,<br>	explained well.9 @ 	Now Moshe and the Levitical priests spoke<br>	to all Israel, saying:<br>	Be silent and hearken, O Israel:<br>	this day you are becoming a people to <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God.10 	You are to hearken to the voice of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,<br>	you are to observe his commandments and his laws that I command you today!11 	And Moshe commanded the people at that time, saying:12 	These you are to stand to bless the people, on Mount Gerizim,<br>	when you have crossed Naftali.14 	And all the Levites are to speak up and say to every man of Israel,<br>	[with] voice raised:15 @ 	Damned be the one<br>	who makes a carved-image or molten-thing, an abomination to <sc>Yhwh</sc>,<br>	made by the hands of an engraver,<br>	and sets [it] up in secret!<br>	And all the people are to speak up and say: Amen!16 @ 	Cursed be<br>	he who insults his father or his leading-astray a blind-person in the way!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!19 @ 	Cursed be<br>	one casting aside the case of a sojourner, an orphan, or a widow!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!20 @ 	Cursed be<br>	one lying with the wife of his father,<br>	for he has exposed the skirt of his father!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!21 @ 	Cursed be<br>	one lying with any animal!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!22 @ 	Cursed be<br>	one lying with his sister,<br>	the daughter of his father or the daughter of his mother!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!23 @ 	Cursed be<br>	one lying with his mother-in-law!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!24 @ 	Cursed be<br>	one striking down his neighbor in secret!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!25 @ 	Cursed be<br>	one taking a bribe,<br>	[thus] striking down a life [through] innocent blood!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!26 @ 	Cursed be<br>	he who does not fulfill the words of this Instruction, to observe them!<br>	And all the people are to say: Amen!28:1 @ 	Now it shall be:<br>	if you hearken, yes, hearken, to the voice of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,<br>	taking care to observe all his commandments that I command you today,<br>	then <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God will make you most-high<br>	above all the nations of the earth.2 	Then there will come upon you all these blessings, and overtake you,<br>	since you have hearkened to the voice of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God:3 	blessed be you, in the town,<br>	blessed be you, in the [open] field;4 	blessed be the fruit of your womb, the fruit of your land, and the fruit of your animals,<br>	the offspring of your cattle and the fecundity of your sheep.5 	Blessed be your basket and your kneading-bowl.6 	Blessed be you, in your coming in,<br>	blessed be you, in your going out.7 	May <sc>Yhwh</sc> make your enemies, those that rise against you,<br>	be defeated before you;<br>	by one road they will go out against you,<br>	but by seven roads they will flee before you.8 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will ordain for you the blessing<br>	in your storehouses,<br>	in all the enterprises of your hand,<br>	and he will bless you in the land that <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God is giving you.9 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will establish you to be a people holy to him,<br>	as he swore to you,<br>	when you keep the commandments of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God<br>	and walk in his ways.10 	And all the peoples of the earth will see<br>	that the name of <sc>Yhwh</sc> is proclaimed over you,<br>	and they will hold you in awe.11 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will leave-excess for you of good-things,<br>	in the fruit of your womb, the fruit of your animals, and the fruit of your land,<br>	on the land that <sc>Yhwh</sc> swore to your fathers, to give them.12 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will open for you his goodly treasuries, the heavens,<br>	by giving the rain of your land in its set-time,<br>	and by blessing all the doings of your hand;<br>	you will lend to many nations,<br>	but you yourself will not have to take-a-loan.13 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will make you the head and not the tail,<br>	you will only be up, you will not be down,<br>	—if you hearken to the commandments of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God<br>	which I command you today, by taking care and by observing [them],14 	that you not turn aside from all the words that I command you today,<br>	to the right or to the left,<br>	by walking after other gods, by serving them.15 @ 	But it shall be:<br>	If you do not hearken to the voice of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,<br>	by taking care and by observing all his commandments and his laws<br>	that I command you today,<br>	then there will come upon you all these curses, and overtake you:16 	cursed be you in the town,<br>	damned be you in the open-field;17 	cursed be your basket and your kneading-bowl,18 	cursed be the fruit of your womb and the fruit of your land,<br>	the offspring of your cattle and the fecundity of your sheep;19 	cursed be you in your coming in,<br>	and damned be you in your going out.20 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will send forth against you<br>	Curse, Bewilderment and Reproach,<br>	against all the enterprises of your hand that you do,<br>	until you are wiped out, until you perish quickly<br>	because of the evil of your deeds by which you have abandoned me.21 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will make the pestilence cling to you,<br>	until it has finished you off from the land that you are entering to possess.22 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will strike you<br>	with consumption, with fever and with inflammation,<br>	with violent-fever and with dehydration,<br>	with blight and with jaundice;<br>	they will pursue you until you perish.23 	The heavens that are above your head will become bronze,<br>	and the earth that is beneath you, iron.24 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will make the rain of your land powder and dust;<br>	from the heavens it will come-down upon you<br>	until you are wiped out.25 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will cause you to be defeated before your enemies:<br>	by one road you will go out against them,<br>	but by seven roads you will flee before them—<br>	you will become an object-of-fright to all the kingdoms of the earth.26 	Your corpse will be for eating<br>	for all the birds of the heavens and for the beasts of the earth,<br>	with none to make [them] tremble.27 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will strike you<br>	with boils of Egypt<br>	and with tumors, with scabs, and with itching,<br>	from which you cannot be healed;28 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will strike you<br>	with madness, with blindness, and with confusion of heart.29 	You will feel about at noon<br>	like a blind-person feels about in deep-darkness,<br>	you will not make your way succeed;<br>	you will be oh so withheld from and robbed all the days,<br>	with no deliverer.30 	A woman you will betroth, but another man will lie with her,<br>	a house you will build, but you will not dwell in it,<br>	a vineyard you will plant, but you will not put-it-to-use,31 	your ox [will be] slaughtered before your eyes, but you will not eat of it,<br>	your donkey will be robbed [from you] in front of you, but it will not return to you,<br>	your sheep will be given to your enemies,<br>	with no deliverer for you.32 	Your sons and your daughters will be given to another people,<br>	while your eyes look on and languish for them all the day,<br>	with no God-power to your hand.33 	The fruit of your land and all that-you-toil-for<br>	will be consumed by a people that you have not known,<br>	you will be only withheld from and downtrodden all the days,34 	and you will go mad from the sight of your eyes that you see!35 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will strike you<br>	with evil boils upon the knees and upon the thighs,<br>	from which you cannot be healed,<br>	from the sole of your foot up to your crown.36 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will drive you and your king whom you have raised over you<br>	to a nation that you have not known, you and your fathers,<br>	and you shall serve there other gods, of wood and of stone.37 	You will become an [example of] desolation, a proverb and a byword<br>	among all the peoples to which <sc>Yhwh</sc> drives you.38 	Much seed will you take out to the field, but little will you gather in,<br>	for locusts will ravage them.39 	Vineyards you will plant and till, but their wine you will not drink, nor will you store [it],<br>	for the worm will devour them.40 	Olive trees you will have throughout all your territory, but oil you will not [get to] pour-for-anointing,<br>	for your olives will drop off.41 	Sons and daughters you will beget, but they will not be yours,<br>	for they will go into captivity.42 	All the trees and the fruit of your soil, the buzzing-cricket will possess.43 	The sojourner who is in your midst<br>	will rise-high above you, higher [and] higher,<br>	while you descend lower and lower;44 	he will lend to you, but you will not lend to him;<br>	he will become the head, but you will become the tail.45 @ 	Now when there come upon you all these curses,<br>	and pursue you and overtake you,<br>	until you have been wiped out,<br>	since you did not hearken to the voice of <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,<br>	to given you.53 	You will consume the fruit of your womb,<br>	the flesh of your sons and of your daughters<br>	that he has given you, <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,<br>	in the siege and in the straits with which your enemy puts-you-in-straits.54 	The softest man among you, the one exceedingly daintiest—<br>	his eye shall be too set-on-evil toward his brother, toward the wife of his bosom,<br>	and toward the rest of his children that he has spared55 	to give to [even] one of them some of the flesh of his children that he eats,<br>	because he has nothing left of anything<br>	in the siege and in the straits with which your enemy puts-you-in-straits, within all your gates.56 	[She] softest among you, the daintiest one,<br>	whose sole of foot has not essayed to be placed upon the earth<br>	out of daintiness and out of being soft—<br>	her eye shall be set-on-evil against the husband of her bosom,<br>	against her son and against her daughter,57 	against her afterbirth that goes out from puts-you-in-straits, within your gates.58 	If you do not carefully observe all the words of this Instruction,<br>	those written in this record,<br>	to hold-in-awe the Name, this honored and awe-inspiring one,<br>	<sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,59 	then <sc>Yhwh</sc> will make-extraordinary the blows [against] you<br>	and the blows [against] your seed,<br>	blows great and lasting,<br>	sicknesses evil and lasting;60 	he will return upon you every illness of Egypt<br>	from which you shrank-in-fear,<br>	so that they cling to you;61 	also every sickness and every blow that is not written in heart, failing eyes and languishing breath.66 	Your life will hang-by-a-thread before you,<br>	you will be terrified night and day,<br>	and you will not trust in [the security of] your life.67 	At daybreak you will say: Who would make it sunset!<br>	And at sunset you will say: Who would make it daybreak!<br>	—out of the terror of your heart that you feel-in-terror,<br>	out of the sight of your eyes that you see.68 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will return you to Egypt in ships,<br>	by the route of which I had said to you:<br>	You shall not see it again any more!<br>	You will put yourselves up for sale there to your enemies as servants and as maids,<br>	with none to buy [you].69 @ 	These are the words of the covenant<br>	that <sc>Yhwh</sc> commanded Moshe to cut with the Children of Israel<br>	in the land of Moav,<br>	aside from the covenant that he cut with them at Horev.29:1 @ 	Moshe called all Israel [together] and said to them:<br>	You yourselves have seen<br>	all that <sc>Yhwh</sc> did anger, wrath, and great fury,<br>	and he cast them into another land, as [is] this day.28 	The hidden things are for <sc>Yhwh</sc> our God,<br>	but the revealed things are for us and for our children, for the ages,<br>	to observe all the words of this Instruction.30:1 @ 	Now it shall be:<br>	when there come upon you all these things,<br>	the blessing and the curse that I have set before be led and bow down to other gods, and serve them,18 	I declare to you today<br>	that you will perish, yes, prish;<br>	you will not prolong days on the land that you are crossing the Jordan to enter, to possess.19 	I call-as-witness against you today the heavens and the earth:<br>	life and death I place before you, blessing and curse;<br>	so choose life, in order that you may stay alive, you and your seed,20 	by loving <sc>Yhwh</sc> your God,<br>	by hearkening to his voice and by cleaving to him,<br>	for he is your life and the length of your days,<br>	to be settled on the land<br>	that <sc>Yhwh</sc> swore to your fathers, to Avraham, to Yitzhak and to Yaakov,<br>	to give them!31:1 @ 	Now Moshe went<br>	and spoke these words to all Israel;2 	he said to them:<br>	A hundred and will cross over before you;<br>	he will wipe out those nations from before you, so that you may dispossess them.<br>	Yehoshua, he will cross over before you,<br>	as <sc>Yhwh</sc> has promised.4 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will do to them<br>	as he did to Sihon and to Og, the kings of the Amorites, and to their land,<br>	that he wiped them out.5 	<sc>Yhwh</sc> will give them before you<br>	and you will
